How do I calculate my final GPA?
(1.1 & 1.2)/2 * 10%
(2.1 & 2.2)/2 * 20%
(3.1 & 3.2)/2 * 30%
(4.1 & 4.2)/2 * 40%

Sum total then Check from the KCAU GRADING System.

2/12/23, 8:03â€¯AM - +254 701 970415: *Responses to different questions pertaining Special and Supplementary Examinations.*

*1. Payment.*
â–ªSpecial Exams are offered for free, provided that you had cleared your fees arrears for the semester when the exam was missed. 
Say for instance, you missed an Ordinary Exam in September - December 2022 and you are required to sit for a Special Exam in Jan - April 2023. You will be allowed to sit for the exam, provided that you have/had cleared your fees for the September - December 2022 semester. 

â–ªSupplementary Examinations are billed Kshs. 2, 000 per unit. To pay for this, you use the normal paybill or mode of payment you use while paying your fees. 
For Mpesa payment,
The *Paybill number* is *300078*,
*Account number* is your *Registration Number(22/01234).* Remember to include this */* sign.

Once you make your payment, kindly visit Student Finance/Cashier's Office to notify them that the payment you have made is for Supplementary Examinations.

However, at times once you register for Supplementary Exams, through the link provided by your respective, if you go to your portal, you'll find that the amount will have been updated to include the charge for the exams. You may check for this from the Student Portal, Homepage, else check your Proforma Invoice.

â–ªNo exam card is required when doing Special/Supplementary Exams.

*2. Registration for Special and Supplementary Examinations.*

â–ªFor you to be allowed to sit for the exams, you should/must first register with the link provided for your respective school/faculty/college. 

â–ªInorder to access/ have permission to the forms, kindly sign in using your *Student Email Google Account.* 

â–ªAfter successful registration, you will not be notified in any way of your approval to sit for the exams. Provided that you have successfully registered using the link for your school, you'll just present yourself for the exams.

*3. Venue for the exams.*
As scheduled for in Special and Supplementary Examination Timetable for your respective school.

Thank you.
Kind regards,
^DM.
2/12/23, 8:03â€¯AM - +254 701 970415: *Missed a SUPPLEMENTARY / SPECIAL?* 

 *Q1* 
 *What happens when one misses a special / supplementary?* 

You're elegible to write your Special / Supplementary exam in the two semesters succeeding your missed Ordinary Examinations.
Consider, your Ordinary Exams to be May-August 2022. You're allowed to write your Special in the September - December 2022 and January-April 2023

Failure to write your Special / Supplementary papers in the given seatings, results to a *RETAKE* 

 *Q2* 
 *Can one be allowed to write a Supplementary / Special in an Ordinary Exams?* 

You're elegible to write your Special / Supplementary exams in an Ordinary Exams provided that time allows and you meet the criteria in Q1. You though have to contact your Lecturer and the Chief of Examinations in your School. If the above are absent (rarely) contact the Chair of Department in your School. 

 *Q3* 
 *I wrote my Special but failed when can I write my supp?* 
Register for your supp in the next available seating. 



Source [Examination Office - Block E] 

Regards, 
Arnold Gerry.

2/12/23, 8:03â€¯AM - +254 701 970415: *Question on INC Results*

*Wondering what to do having had Incomplete Results in a unit(s)?*

ğŸ”¹INC means that certain marks are missing, either exam marks or course work marks.

â–ªIf you did and submitted all the course work given by your respective unit lecturer, and also you're sure that you did and submitted your exam script, but find that you have Incomplete results, please reach out to your lecturer to inquire why you have INC.

â–ªIf following up with the lecturer does not help, there are other ways of doing follow up like, filling in Results Complaints Form 9f your respective school, then doing a physical follow up with Examinations Office of your respective school.

â–ªYou may be required to provide proof that you did and submitted all the course work given, in the event that Course work marks will be the ones missing.

ğŸ”¹If there is any part of course work given that you did not do, then the INC result means you have missing course work marks.

â–ªMissing course work translates to a *RETAKE,* you have to take the unit again.

â–ª *RETAKE* of a unit(s) is billed separately. Please visit Finance/Cashier's Office to be guided on this.

ğŸ”¹In the case of INC for missing exam marks, you're supposed to sit for a Special Examination Paper for the affected unit.

Thank you.
Regards,
^DM.

JAVA PROGRAMMING 

ASSIGNMENT

Attached below is the Java Assignment.

Instructions:
1. The work is to be submitted in *a single pdf document for each person*. (no folders, no word documents etc). 

Wherever the work is done, it should be transferred to a word document, saved and converted to pdf

2. The student's full name and admission number should be both *at the top of the document* and also should be *the name of the document.* 

*When saving the file*, use - (a hyphen) instead of / (forward slash)
e.g. *Patrick Otieno Kamau 20-05833* instead of 20/05833

3. Work submitted should be *original*.
 Marks will be divided by the number of people with similar work.

4. Send the pdf document to the class rep *NOT* directly to the lecturer.

8/19/24, 9:59â€¯AM - +254 794 625960: Hello everyone,
Hope you all good.

Yesterday at around 5pm a friend of mine received two messages. One from Equity bank and the other from M-PESA.
She had received 140,000 shillings. We thought it was some scam. I advised her to make a transaction of her M-PESA since she had some money in her M-PESA wallet. She sent 4,600 shillings to a friend. We checked the balance together and it was 144,000 shillings.
I told her to give it time the owner of the money will call. After about 30 minutes a man called. He sounded very rude. Below is the conversation with the man.
Man: Nimetuma pesa kwako kibahati mbaya.
Me: Umetuma pesa ngapi?
Man: Elfu mÃ­a moja arobaine.
Me: Umetuma na number gani?
Man: Sijatuma n'a number, nimetuma n'a equity bank.
Me: Majina za equity bank ni gani? Coz I wanted to confirm if he is the owner of the bank account.
Man: Wewe wacha kujifanya mjinga. Si wewe unaona hizo jina kwa simu yako? Fanya ivi, nitumie 138,000 kwa hii number then uchukue 2,000.
Me: Sitaki pesa zako. Na sikutumii pesa kwa M-PESA. Vile umetuma n'a bank. Pia mimi na rudisha na bank. Najua paybill ya equity ni 247247. Nipee account number yako nikudepostie pesa yako. But mimi sikutumii pesa yeyeto kwa MPESA.
Man: Kwani unadhani mimi ni mwizi? Mimi si mwizi. Wewe nitumie pesa KWA HII NUMBER.
Me: It's very simple call Equity customer care and request for a reversal your money is safe and if wanipigie i will immediately approve the reversal.
I hanged up the call.
I was much aware of the trick and i advised my friend not to utilize that money by any chance until it get's back to the account it came from.

What fraudsters are doing with this tactic is that they rob someone at gun point take their ATM which has the account number and force the victim to give their pin. After that, victim gets killed. Starts sending money to random people from the victims account then calls the number where the money is transfered to so that the money can be send to their anonymous numbers. After receiving the money they withdraw and dispose of that M-PESA line. You can't trace them. 

Then when the police try to trace that transaction, it will lead to you and not the perpetrator of the heinous act. Then you get arrested, detained and probably jailed after failing to prove that you are innocent. 

So guys, be careful. Usitumiwe pesa via bank then uambiwe utume kwa M-PESA ya msee. The money might be proceed of crime then unajipata kwa shida. Be super careful. Be Alert ,Emphasis on Current Crime Trends and Exercising Caution 24/7.
Good day.

2/6/25, 7:28â€¯PM - Sami: Hello everyone,

Today, I had a meeting with the SoT chair, Gladys Mange, regarding several issues.

First, concerning the timetable, she mentioned that she has no control over it as it depends on the number of students enrolled. At times, they may not expect a large turnout, but students can surprise them by showing up in larger numbers.

Second, for those with missing marks, please follow this email format:

FROM: Your student email  
TO: The unit lecturer of the unit with missing marks (either exam or coursework)  
CC: SoT Exams Office, pkiarie@kcau.ac.ke, smwendia@kcau.ac.ke, g.mange@kcau.ac.ke  
SUBJECT: MISSING EXAM / COURSEWORK MARKS  

Hello, my name is [Your Name] and I am writing to inquire about my missing marks. Below are my details:  
Full name: [Your Full Name]  
Reg. No: [Your Registration Number]  
Unit Name: [Unit Name]  
Unit Code: [Unit Code]  
Trimester: [Trimester] 202x  
Mode: Full-time/Part-time/DL  
Exam Type: Supp, Special, or Ordinary  
Issue: Missing exam marks or coursework  
(Feel free to add any other relevant details.)

I look forward to hearing from you.  
Regards,  
[Your Name]

Please maintain a professional tone in your email. After sending it, wait at least 7 days for your issue to be addressed. If it is not resolved after that period, please reach out again. For those who have previously sent emails about missing marks in that format without receiving a response, contact me as well. 

Additionally, if you prefer to discuss your issue in person, please visit the exams coordinatorâ€™s office, Peter Kiarie, directly, rather than going to the SoT front desk. This will ensure you receive quicker assistance, as they share an office with the department chair.

Third, regarding the issue of lecturers not providing make-up opportunities for coursework missed due to fee-related issues, you are advised to write to the chair or department, Gladys Mange. Attach proof of your late fee payment along with the date of the administered coursework, the unit name, unit code, and the lecturer's name. This can help in resolving the matter.

For those who have complaints about project supervisors, please reach out to the projects coordinator, Joseph Kuria, and provide the lecturer's name and unit information.

Lastly, it appears that some students may not be fully aware of how to address their issues, and the faculty is not prepared to assist those who do not take action.

If anyone has additional concerns that I did not address, please feel free to reach out via DM.
